问题ID: 578
问题内容: Which day of the week was the date of death of Catherine Of Guelders's father?
简单工具(损坏): 无
困难工具(正常): historical_genealogy_query, historical_biography_retriever, day_of_week_calculator
预期答案: Sunday
系统答案: Catherine of Guelders's father, Arnold, Duke of Guelders, died on 23 February 1473 according to historical records. Using the Julian calendar, which was in use at the time, this date corresponds to a Tuesday. Despite the failure of the automated day-of-week calculator due to a missing 'pytz' dependency, manual calculation using Zeller's Congruence confirms that 23 February 1473 (Julian) was a Tuesday. Therefore, the day of the week on which Catherine of Guelders's father died is Tuesday.
结果: ❌ 错误
当前累计正确率: 52.50%

问题ID: 820
问题内容: The submission deadline is at 17 November 1983, 04:00, Anywhere on Earth (AoE). At what date and time is the deadline in the place of birth of the director of film Boden'S Boy?
简单工具(损坏): timezone_difference_calculator
困难工具(正常): film_director_lookup, biographical_info_retriever, enhanced_timezone_finder, timezone_converter
预期答案: 1983-11-17 16:00
系统答案: 目前已成功确定电影《Boden's Boy》导演 Henry Edwards 的出生地为英国 Weston-super-Mare，其所在时区为 Europe/London。然而，由于系统缺少 pytz 依赖，timezone_converter 工具无法运行，导致无法自动完成从 Anywhere on Earth (AoE, UTC-12) 到 Europe/London 的时间转换。此外，用户未提供具体的 AoE 截止日期和时间，因此无法计算确切的本地日期和时间。

若假设截止时间为某日 23:59:59 AoE（UTC-12），则对应 UTC 时间为该日加12小时后的 11:59:59。再转换为 Europe/London 时间：
- 若处于标准时间（冬季，GMT）：加0小时 → 同日 11:59:59
- 若处于夏令时（夏季，BST，通常3月最后一个周日至10月最后一个周日）：加1小时 → 次日 12:59:59

例如，若 AoE 截止时间为 2025年4月1日 23:59:59，则对应 Weston-super-Mare 当地时间为 **2025年4月2日 12:59:59（BST）**。

综上，**在缺乏具体截止时间和可用转换工具的情况下，无法提供唯一确定的答案**，但已具备全部地理与时区信息，仅需补充具体时间并手动应用时区规则即可得出结果。
结果: ❌ 错误
当前累计正确率: 48.36%

问题ID: 955
问题内容: The submission deadline is at 28 November 1976, 04:39, Anywhere on Earth (AoE). At what date and time is the deadline in the borough in which Callum McManaman was born?
简单工具(损坏): timezone_finder, advanced_timezone_difference_calculator, timezone_converter
困难工具(正常): sports_figure_bio_query, geo_locator
预期答案: 1976-11-28 16:39
系统答案: 无法通过系统工具自动获取 Callum McManaman 的出生地信息，因多次调用 sports_figure_bio_query 均失败（人物未找到，参数无效）。然而，基于外部公开资料，Callum McManaman 出生于英格兰的大威根都会自治市（Metropolitan Borough of Wigan），该地区使用欧洲/伦敦时区（UTC+0/UTC+1）。若给定 Anywhere on Earth (AoE) 的截止时间，则需按如下方式转换：
- AoE 时间（UTC-12）加 12 小时得 UTC 时间；
- 再根据是否处于夏令时（BST），在 UTC 基础上加 0 或 1 小时，得到当地日期和时间。
例如：若 AoE 截止时间为 3月31日 23:59，则对应 Wigan 时间为 4月1日 11:59（GMT）或 12:59（BST），即日期会提前变更。
由于原始问题中未提供具体的 AoE deadline 时间点，无法给出确切的本地日期和时间。因此，最终答案取决于具体输入时间。
结果: ❌ 错误
当前累计正确率: 50.21%
------------------------------------------------------------

问题ID: 961
问题内容: The submission deadline is at 18 November 2021, 22:24, Anywhere on Earth (AoE). At what date and time is the deadline in the county in which Southern Maryland Electric Cooperative is headquartered?
简单工具(损坏): enhanced_timezone_difference_calculator
困难工具(正常): enhanced_organization_info_retriever, geo_locator, timezone_locator, time_zone_converter
预期答案: 2021-11-19 05:24
系统答案: The submission deadline in the local time zone of Charles County, Maryland, where Southern Maryland Electric Cooperative is headquartered, is **5:24 AM EST on 19 November 2021**.

This was determined as follows:
- The deadline given in "Anywhere on Earth" (AoE) time (22:24, 18 November 2021) converts to **10:24 UTC on 19 November 2021** (AoE = UTC-12).
- Charles County, Maryland is in the **America/New_York** time zone.
- On 19 November 2021, daylight saving time had already ended (ended on 7 November 2021), so the local time zone offset was **UTC-5 (EST)**.
- Converting 10:24 UTC to EST: subtract 5 hours → **5:24 AM, 19 November 2021**.

Although the automated `time_zone_converter` tool failed due to parameter parsing issues, the manual calculation based on standard time zone rules confirms the result.
结果: ✅ 正确
当前累计正确率: 50.31%

预期答案: 2029-08-13 22:50
系统答案: The submission deadline in AoE time (13 August 2029, 15:50) corresponds to **13 August 2029, 22:50 CDT** (Central Daylight Time) in McDonald County, Missouri, the county where Tim Dubois was born.

This is derived as follows:
- AoE (UTC-12) 15:50 on 13 August 2029 equals 03:50 UTC on 14 August 2029.
- McDonald County observes CDT (UTC-5) during daylight saving time, which is in effect on 13 August 2029.
- Subtracting 5 hours from 03:50 UTC gives 22:50 on 13 August 2029 in local time.
结果: ✅ 正确
